msg:The Shangri-La, Tianjin, is, and has always been our favorite Hotel to visit.

This week was a special celebration for us, as we celebrated our 15th Wedding anniversary, as well as our 4th consecutive year in China.

We relocated to another City / Province, about two years ago, and was unable to visit and enjoy our special Shangri-La.

Prior to us moving from Tianjin, we used to celebrate all our special occasions and milestones, at this branch of Shangri-La.

We would always spend our Christmas, New Years, and Chinese New Year's at Shangri-La.

Now that we have returned to Heibei, we look forward to continuing this tradition.

Things change over time, some familiar faces are no longer working there.

However, the new team made us feel right at home again, and went out of their way to make our stay most memorable and special.

As I mentioned to one of the team members, it's not the spectacular Lobby Lounge, nor the beautifully decorated features, that make the establishment, but rather the people.

Without quality staff and superior service, no establishment can ever rely on reoccurring business.

For as long as these values are in place, this Shangri-La can be certain of our patronage.

All team members provided excellent service, from the bellhop, to the waitresses, from the front of house to the housekeeping and of course the management team.

Special thanks to "Francis", the new General Manager, "Danny", the Food and Beverage Director, as well as "Billy", the "Food and Beverage" Manager.

This trio of Management, ensured that we received the best service possible.

Lastly, we would like to thank "Roger" whom assisted us with a Driver / Transportation, upon our early departure.

No visit to Tianjin, would ever truly be complete, with visiting The Shangri-La.

See you soon.

msg:The hotel is in a great location. It only takes one stop to get off at Dawangzhuang Station after exiting Tianjin Station. There are Kerry Plaza and Jinhui Bridge nearby, which are very convenient for shopping and traveling. The rooms and hotel facilities are well maintained, especially the Haihe River view in the room should be one of the best in Tianjin.
The staff are very friendly, including Ms. Ruby at the front desk who introduced various services very carefully, the lounge staff answered questions and cleaned seats in a timely manner, and the aunt and uncle of the room service were very polite and enthusiastic in the elevator and when delivering items, etc., thank you!
Overall, it was a perfect stay with no shortcomings. It would be better if the restaurant and lounge breakfast could be richer and dishes could be added in time when it was about to end but not yet ended.

Yun Coffee Buffet Dinner: Nice environment, good service, rich dishes, and good quality. Maybe there will be more choices if you go to Kerry Plaza next door.

It is very pleasant. The hotel rooms are clean and spacious, with complete facilities, and the catering - whether it is seafood buffet or Shang Palace self-ordering, is rich and varied, and of high quality. msg:Allow me to press Amway Shangri-La again.
My husband and I's favorite hotel brand. Five-star brand hotels, except for the Four Seasons, have basically experienced the rest. There are not 100 large and medium-sized cities at home and abroad, but dozens of them. Shangri-La's quality is one of a kind, impeccable.

Room Facilities:
Shangri-La's room is not the largest among the five-star hotels, but it is definitely the warmest, and it feels like home when entering. From bedding, home appliance curtains, to bathroom washing, tea bar and minibar, the details are really in place.

Value for money:
In a five-star hotel, the price/performance ratio is very high. Compared with some first-tier high-end brand hotels in the group, it is really a civilian price.

breakfast:
The Shangri-La breakfast in each city will arrange local specialty snacks. As a Tianjin native, I ate Shangri-La Tianjin specialty snacks. I know that the special snacks and breakfasts in other cities are very authentic.

wifi:
Seek truth from facts, this is general.

bed:
It's worth mentioning that the firmness of the bed really suits me. I don't like too soft beds.

parking:
convenient.

Room View:
As shown.

Serve:
This must be praised. Of all the big-name hotels I've stayed in, including the Ritz-Carlton, only Shangri-La calls before check-in to ask about accommodation preferences and needs, and then calls the next day after check-out to ask questions and comments about the accommodation. For this serious attitude, it is worth five points. Besides the service of the waiters, from the concierge room at the front desk to the gymnasium of the Horizon Club restaurant, all the waiters serve customers in the principle of meeting all reasonable requirements of customers. However, the bad thing about this check-in experience is that the little brother who spread pancakes and fruits in the restaurant in the morning, I don't know if I didn't have a good dream yesterday or I got up. The attitude is blunt and the tone is not good, which is offensive.

This time I booked the Horizon Club River View Room, which has a capsule machine and a free minibar. There are also flowers, fruit wine and chocolate. Including afternoon tea and happy hour at the Horizon Club on the 32nd floor. Needless to say, basically three meals a day can be solved in the hotel. During the epidemic, it's nice to come and relax occasionally.
